    <!-- FOOTER -->
    <script type="text/javascript">
     function OpenrChatOnline() {
        var ifrm = document.createElement("iframe");
        ifrm.setAttribute("src", "https://ca.socialgateway.net/webchat/website/ping?style=friendly&hideCloseBtn=true");
        ifrm.setAttribute("runat", "server");
        ifrm.setAttribute("id", "asistenteFrame");
        document.getElementById("chatonline-wrapper").appendChild(ifrm);
        if ($('[id*="chkChatonline"]').val() == "true" && !$("#chatonline-wrapper").is(':visible') ) {
            $("#chatonline-wrapper").show();
        }
    }

    function CerrarChatOnline() {
        if ($('[id*="chkChatonline"]').val() == "true") {
            $('[id*="chkChatonline"]').val("false");
            var asistenteFrame = document.getElementById('asistenteFrame');
            asistenteFrame.parentNode.removeChild(asistenteFrame);
        }
        else {
            $('[id*="chkChatonline"]').val("true");
        }
        $('[id*="btnChatonline"]').click();
    }
    </script>

          {
            return 'WPHONE';
          }
          else

                }
            }



            /* Open popup */
            if (iostype != "UNKNOWN") {
              $(popup).show();
            }else{
                $("#popup-app").hide();
            }

            /* Close popup if user clicks on background */
            $(popup).click(function(e) {
                if ( e.target == this ) {
                    if ($(popup).is(':visible')) {
                        $(popup).hide();
                    }
                }
            });

            /* Close popup and remove errors if user clicks on cancel or close buttons */
            $(popup).find("button[name=close-pop]").on("click", function() {
                $(popup).hide();
            });
        }
    }

            $('#btnCargarGrilla').click();

        function focustxtBuscador() {
            var $field = $("#txtBuscador").val();
            setTimeout(function () {
                var $field = $("#txtBuscador"),
                oldVal = $field.val();
                $field.focus().val('').val(oldVal);
            }, 5);
        }

        });

        $(document).ready(function(){
            setInterval(bannerSlideShow, 5000);

        var quotes = [
            "/img/miniban/mini180x100_01_es.png",
            "/img/miniban/mini180x100_02_es.png",
            "/img/miniban/mini180x100_02_es.png",
            "/img/miniban/mini180x100_01_es.png"

        ];
        var aeropuntosES = [
            "/img/miniban/banner-aeropuntos-02-es.png",
            "/img/miniban/banner-aeropuntos-03-es.png",
            "/img/miniban/banner-aeropuntos-01-es.png"
        ];
        var aeropuntosEN = [
            "/img/miniban/banner-aeropuntos-02-en.png",
            "/img/miniban/banner-aeropuntos-03-en.png",
            "/img/miniban/banner-aeropuntos-01-en.png"
        ];
        var i = 0;
        var y = 0;
        function bannerSlideShow() {
            document.getElementById("miniban-rotator").src = quotes[i];
            idioma = $('[id*="lblIdiomaForPopUp"]').text();
            if (idioma == 'ES-AR'){
            	document.getElementById("miniban-rotator-aeropuntos").src = aeropuntosES[y];
            }else{
            	document.getElementById("miniban-rotator-aeropuntos").src = aeropuntosEN[y];
            }
            if (i < (quotes.length-1)) {i++;}
            else {i = 0;}

            if (y < (aeropuntosES.length-1)) {y++;}
            else {y = 0;}
        }
